Perfect! Now let me create one final summary showing all findings:

---

## 📋 COMPREHENSIVE INVESTIGATION SUMMARY

I've thoroughly investigated the Max codebase. Here are my **detailed findings** across all areas:

### **1. TUI IMPLEMENTATION** ✅

**Framework**: Node.js built-in `readline` module (NOT ink, blessed, or other TUI libraries)
- **File**: `/Users/burkeholland/dev/max/src/tui/index.ts` (922 lines)
- **Architecture**: Pure terminal I/O + SSE streaming
- **Key Components**:
  - **Readline interface** (Line 329-335): Handles line input, history (1000 max lines)
  - **Keypress handler** (Line 783): Detects Escape key to cancel responses
  - **Input handler** (Line 790): Processes user input, parses commands
  - **SSE connection** (Line 376-495): Real-time streaming via HTTP Server-Sent Events
  - **Markdown renderer** (Line 72-230): Converts markdown to ANSI for terminal display
  - **Command handlers** (Line 643-770): `/model`, `/memory`, `/skills`, `/workers`, `/copy`, `/status`, `/restart`, `/clear`, `/quit`

**Message Flow**: User Input → Readline → HTTP POST `/message` → API → Orchestrator → SDK → Model → SSE Stream back to TUI

### **2. ORCHESTRATOR/COPILOT** ✅

**File**: `/Users/burkeholland/dev/max/src/copilot/orchestrator.ts` (414 lines)
- **Architecture**: Single persistent session with message queue (serialized FIFO)
- **Current Message Format**: Text-only
  ```typescript
  // Line 276: Current send
  const result = await session.sendAndWait({ prompt }, 300_000);
  ```
- **Message Tagging**: Prompts tagged with source `[via tui]`, `[via telegram]`, or `[via background]`
- **Response Streaming**: Accumulates message_delta events, streams via callback
- **Session Persistence**: Session ID saved to SQLite, resumed on restart (Line 163-186)
- **Retry Logic**: 3 attempts with exponential backoff on connection errors (Line 350-385)

**Key Limitation**: Currently passes only `prompt` to SDK, **no attachments parameter**

### **3. COPILOT SDK CAPABILITIES** ✅✅✅

**Version**: `@github/copilot-sdk@0.1.26` (in package.json)
- **Full Image Support Available**: YES! The SDK's `MessageOptions` interface supports attachments
- **Type Definition** (types.d.ts:643-676):
  ```typescript
  export interface MessageOptions {
    prompt: string;
    attachments?: Array\<{
      type: "file";
      path: string;
      displayName?: string;
    } | {
      type: "directory";
      path: string;
      displayName?: string;
    } | {
      type: "selection";
      filePath: string;
      displayName: string;
      selection?: { start, end };
      text?: string;
    }\>;
    mode?: "enqueue" | "immediate";
  }
  ```
- **Supported Image Formats**: JPG, PNG, GIF, WebP, BMP (per README)
- **Model Vision Capability**: Declared in RPC definitions
  ```typescript
  capabilities: {
    supports: {
      vision: boolean;  // ← Models declare this
      reasoningEffort: boolean;
    };
  }
  ```
- **How SDK Uses It**: Takes file path, reads from disk, encodes internally, sends to model

### **4. EXISTING IMAGE HANDLING** ❌

**Search Results**: Only 1 image reference in entire codebase
- **Location**: `/Users/burkeholland/dev/max/src/copilot/system-message.ts` (Line 128)
- **Content**: Instructions for sending photos TO Telegram (outbound only)
  ```
  curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:7777/send-photo -d '{"photo": "\<path\>", "caption": "\<optional\>"}'
  ```
- **No other references** to: `image_url`, `multipart`, `base64`, `clipboard paste`, `vision`, or image input

**Existing Image Tech**:
- ✅ Clipboard COPY for responses (pbcopy/xclip/xsel)
- ❌ Clipboard PASTE for images
- ❌ Image attachment from TUI
- ❌ Image drag-and-drop
- ❌ Base64 encoding

### **5. INPUT HANDLING** ✅

**Keyboard Capture**:
- **Escape key**: Detected via `process.stdin.on("keypress", ...)` (Line 783) → calls `sendCancel()`
- **Text input**: `rl.on("line", (line) =\> ...)` (Line 790) → captures user input after Enter
- **History**: Builtin readline history + persistent file (Line 329-335, 289-315)
- **Navigation**: Up/Down arrows work via readline, Enter submits, Ctrl+C interrupts (readline defaults)

**Terminal Library**: Pure Node.js, no external TUI frameworks
- Input source: `process.stdin` (raw terminal)
- Output sink: `process.stdout` (ANSI codes manually written)
- Columns detection: `process.stdout.columns || 80`

**NO Paste Handling**: 
- No stdin paste listener
- No clipboard image read capability
- Could be added but not currently implemented

### **6. DEPENDENCIES** ✅

**package.json Analysis**:
```json
{
  "dependencies": {
    "@github/copilot-sdk": "^0.1.26",   // ✅ Supports attachments/images

96.

1. import { approveAll, type CopilotClient, type CopilotSession } from "@github/copilot-sdk";
2. import { createTools, type WorkerInfo } from "./tools.js";
3. import { getOrchestratorSystemMessage } from "./system-message.js";

11. const MAX_RETRIES = 3;
12. const RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS = [1_000, 3_000, 10_000];

15. const ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY = "orchestrator_session_id";

17. export type MessageSource =
18.   | { type: "telegram"; chatId: number; messageId: number }
19.   | { type: "tui"; connectionId: string }
20.   | { type: "background" };
21. 
22. export type MessageCallback = (text: string, done: boolean) => void;
23. 
24. type LogFn = (direction: "in" | "out", source: string, text: string) => void;
25. let logMessage: LogFn = () => {};
26. 
27. export function setMessageLogger(fn: LogFn): void {
28.   logMessage = fn;
29. }

31. // Proactive notification — sends unsolicited messages to the user on a specific channel
32. type ProactiveNotifyFn = (text: string, channel?: "telegram" | "tui") => void;
33. let proactiveNotifyFn: ProactiveNotifyFn | undefined;
34. 
35. export function setProactiveNotify(fn: ProactiveNotifyFn): void {
36.   proactiveNotifyFn = fn;
37. }

39. let copilotClient: CopilotClient | undefined;
40. const workers = new Map<string, WorkerInfo>();

48. // Message queue — serializes access to the single persistent session
49. type QueuedMessage = {
50.   prompt: string;
51.   callback: MessageCallback;
52.   sourceChannel?: "telegram" | "tui";
53.   resolve: (value: string) => void;
54.   reject: (err: unknown) => void;

61.

67. function getSessionConfig() {
68.   const tools = createTools({
69.     client: copilotClient!,
70.     workers,
71.     onWorkerComplete: feedBackgroundResult,
72.   });
73.   const mcpServers = loadMcpConfig();
74.   const skillDirectories = getSkillDirectories();

78. /** Feed a background worker result into the orchestrator as a new turn. */
79. export function feedBackgroundResult(workerName: string, result: string): void {
80.   const worker = workers.get(workerName);
81.   const channel = worker?.originChannel;
82.   const prompt = `[Background task completed] Worker '${workerName}' finished:\n\n${result}`;
83.   sendToOrchestrator(
84.     prompt,
85.     { type: "background" },
86.     (_text, done) => {
87.       if (done && proactiveNotifyFn) {
88.         proactiveNotifyFn(_text, channel);
89.       }
90.     }
91.   );
92. }

94. function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
95.   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
96. }

98. /** Ensure the SDK client is connected, resetting if necessary. Coalesces concurrent resets. */
99. let resetPromise: Promise<CopilotClient> | undefined;
100. async function ensureClient(): Promise<CopilotClient> {
101.   if (copilotClient && copilotClient.getState() === "connected") {
102.     return copilotClient;
103.   }
104.   if (!resetPromise) {
105.     console.log(`[max] Client not connected (state: ${copilotClient?.getState() ?? "null"}), resetting…`);
106.     resetPromise = resetClient().then((c) => {
107.       console.log(`[max] Client reset successful, state: ${c.getState()}`);
108.       copilotClient = c;
109.       return c;
110.     }).finally(() => { resetPromise = undefined; });
111.   }
112.   return resetPromise;
113. }
114. 
115. /** Start periodic health check that proactively reconnects the client. */
116. function startHealthCheck(): void {
117.   if (healthCheckTimer) return;
118.   healthCheckTimer = setInterval(async () => {
119.     if (!copilotClient) return;
120.     try {
121.       const state = copilotClient.getState();
122.       if (state !== "connected") {
123.         console.log(`[max] Health check: client state is '${state}', resetting…`);
124.         await ensureClient();
125.         // Session may need recovery after client reset
126.         orchestratorSession = undefined;
127.       }
128.     } catch (err) {
129.       console.error(`[max] Health check error:`, err instanceof Error ? err.message : err);
130.     }
131.   }, HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL_MS);
132. }
133. 
134. /** Create or resume the persistent orchestrator session. */
135. async function ensureOrchestratorSession(): Promise<CopilotSession> {
136.   if (orchestratorSession) return orchestratorSession;
137.   // Coalesce concurrent callers — wait for an in-flight creation
138.   if (sessionCreatePromise) return sessionCreatePromise;
139. 
140.   sessionCreatePromise = createOrResumeSession();
141.   try {
142.     const session = await sessionCreatePromise;
143.     orchestratorSession = session;
144.     return session;
145.   } finally {
146.     sessionCreatePromise = undefined;
147.   }
148. }
149. 
150. /** Internal: actually create or resume a session (not concurrency-safe — use ensureOrchestratorSession). */
151. async function createOrResumeSession(): Promise<CopilotSession> {
152.   const client = await ensureClient();
153.   const { tools, mcpServers, skillDirectories } = getSessionConfig();
154.   const memorySummary = getMemorySummary();
155. 
156.   const infiniteSessions = {
157.     enabled: true,
158.     backgroundCompactionThreshold: 0.80,
159.     bufferExhaustionThreshold: 0.95,
160.   };
161. 
162.   // Try to resume a previous session
163.   const savedSessionId = getState(ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY);
164.   if (savedSessionId) {
165.     try {
166.       console.log(`[max] Resuming orchestrator session ${savedSessionId.slice(0, 8)}…`);
167.       const session = await client.resumeSession(savedSessionId, {
168.         model: config.copilotModel,
169.         configDir: SESSIONS_DIR,
170.         streaming: true,
171.         systemMessage: {
172.           content: getOrchestratorSystemMessage(memorySummary || undefined, { selfEditEnabled: config.selfEditEnabled }),
173.         },
174.         tools,
175.         mcpServers,
176.         skillDirectories,
177.         onPermissionRequest: approveAll,
178.         infiniteSessions,
179.       });
180.       console.log(`[max] Resumed orchestrator session successfully`);
181.       return session;
182.     } catch (err) {
183.       console.log(`[max] Could not resume session: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : err}. Creating new.`);
184.       deleteState(ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY);
185.     }
186.   }
187. 
188.   // Create a fresh session
189.   console.log(`[max] Creating new persistent orchestrator session`);
190.   const session = await client.createSession({
191.     model: config.copilotModel,
192.     configDir: SESSIONS_DIR,
193.     streaming: true,
194.     systemMessage: {
195.       content: getOrchestratorSystemMessage(memorySummary || undefined, { selfEditEnabled: config.selfEditEnabled }),
196.     },
197.     tools,
198.     mcpServers,
199.     skillDirectories,
200.     onPermissionRequest: approveAll,
201.     infiniteSessions,
202.   });
203. 
204.   // Persist the session ID for future restarts
205.   setState(ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY, session.sessionId);
206.   console.log(`[max] Created orchestrator session ${session.sessionId.slice(0, 8)}…`);
207. 
208.   // Recover conversation context if available (session was lost, not first run)
209.   const recentHistory = getRecentConversation(10);
210.   if (recentHistory) {
211.     console.log(`[max] Injecting recent conversation context into new session`);
212.     try {
213.       await session.sendAndWait({
214.         prompt: `[System: Session recovered] Your previous session was lost. Here's the recent conversation for context — do NOT respond to these messages, just absorb the context silently:\n\n${recentHistory}\n\n(End of recovery context. Wait for the next real message.)`,
215.       }, 60_000);
216.     } catch (err) {
217.       console.log(`[max] Context recovery injection failed (non-fatal): ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : err}`);
218.     }
219.   }
220. 
221.   return session;
222. }
223. 
224. export async function initOrchestrator(client: CopilotClient): Promise<void> {
225.   copilotClient = client;
226.   const { mcpServers, skillDirectories } = getSessionConfig();
227. 
228.   // Validate configured model against available models
229.   try {
230.     const models = await client.listModels();
231.     const configured = config.copilotModel;
232.     const isAvailable = models.some((m) => m.id === configured);
233.     if (!isAvailable) {
234.       console.log(`[max] ⚠️ Configured model '${configured}' is not available. Falling back to '${DEFAULT_MODEL}'.`);
235.       config.copilotModel = DEFAULT_MODEL;
236.     }
237.   } catch (err) {
238.     console.log(`[max] Could not validate model (will use '${config.copilotModel}' as-is): ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : err}`);
239.   }
240. 
241.   console.log(`[max] Loading ${Object.keys(mcpServers).length} MCP server(s): ${Object.keys(mcpServers).join(", ") || "(none)"}`);
242.   console.log(`[max] Skill directories: ${skillDirectories.join(", ") || "(none)"}`);
243.   console.log(`[max] Persistent session mode — conversation history maintained by SDK`);
244.   startHealthCheck();
245. 
246.   // Eagerly create/resume the orchestrator session
247.   try {
248.     await ensureOrchestratorSession();
249.   } catch (err) {
250.     console.error(`[max] Failed to create initial session (will retry on first message):`, err instanceof Error ? err.message : err);
251.   }
252. }
253. 
254. /** Send a prompt on the persistent session, return the response. */
255. async function executeOnSession(prompt: string, callback: MessageCallback): Promise<string> {
256.   const session = await ensureOrchestratorSession();
257.   currentCallback = callback;
258. 
259.   let accumulated = "";
260.   let toolCallExecuted = false;
261.   const unsubToolDone = session.on("tool.execution_complete", () => {
262.     toolCallExecuted = true;
263.   });
264.   const unsubDelta = session.on("assistant.message_delta", (event) => {
265.     // After a tool call completes, ensure a line break separates the text blocks
266.     // so they don't visually run together in the TUI.
267.     if (toolCallExecuted && accumulated.length > 0 && !accumulated.endsWith("\n")) {
268.       accumulated += "\n";
269.     }
270.     toolCallExecuted = false;
271.     accumulated += event.data.deltaContent;
272.     callback(accumulated, false);
273.   });
274. 
275.   try {
276.     const result = await session.sendAndWait({ prompt }, 300_000);
277.     const finalContent = result?.data?.content || accumulated || "(No response)";
278.     return finalContent;
279.   } catch (err) {
280.     // If the session is broken, invalidate it so it's recreated on next attempt
281.     const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
282.     if (/closed|destroy|disposed|invalid|expired|not found/i.test(msg)) {
283.       console.log(`[max] Session appears dead, will recreate: ${msg}`);
284.       orchestratorSession = undefined;
285.       deleteState(ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY);
286.     }
287.     throw err;
288.   } finally {
289.     unsubDelta();
290.     unsubToolDone();
291.     currentCallback = undefined;
292.   }
293. }
294. 
295. /** Process the message queue one at a time. */
296. async function processQueue(): Promise<void> {
297.   if (processing) {
298.     if (messageQueue.length > 0) {
299.       console.log(`[max] Message queued (${messageQueue.length} waiting — orchestrator is busy)`);
300.     }
301.     return;
302.   }
303.   processing = true;
304. 
305.   while (messageQueue.length > 0) {
306.     const item = messageQueue.shift()!;
307.     currentSourceChannel = item.sourceChannel;
308.     try {
309.       const result = await executeOnSession(item.prompt, item.callback);
310.       item.resolve(result);
311.     } catch (err) {
312.       item.reject(err);
313.     }
314.     currentSourceChannel = undefined;
315.   }
316. 
317.   processing = false;
318. }
319. 
320. function isRecoverableError(err: unknown): boolean {
321.   const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
322.   return /timeout|disconnect|connection|EPIPE|ECONNRESET|ECONNREFUSED|socket|closed|ENOENT|spawn|not found|expired|stale/i.test(msg);
323. }
324. 
325. export async function sendToOrchestrator(
326.   prompt: string,
327.   source: MessageSource,
328.   callback: MessageCallback
329. ): Promise<void> {
330.   const sourceLabel =
331.     source.type === "telegram" ? "telegram" :
332.     source.type === "tui" ? "tui" : "background";
333.   logMessage("in", sourceLabel, prompt);
334. 
335.   // Tag the prompt with its source channel
336.   const taggedPrompt = source.type === "background"
337.     ? prompt
338.     : `[via ${sourceLabel}] ${prompt}`;
339. 
340.   // Log role: background events are "system", user messages are "user"
341.   const logRole = source.type === "background" ? "system" : "user";
342. 
343.   // Determine the source channel for worker origin tracking
344.   const sourceChannel: "telegram" | "tui" | undefined =
345.     source.type === "telegram" ? "telegram" :
346.     source.type === "tui" ? "tui" : undefined;
347. 
348.   // Enqueue and process
349.   void (async () => {
350.     for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= MAX_RETRIES; attempt++) {
351.       try {
352.         const finalContent = await new Promise<string>((resolve, reject) => {
353.           messageQueue.push({ prompt: taggedPrompt, callback, sourceChannel, resolve, reject });
354.           processQueue();
355.         });
356.         // Deliver response to user FIRST, then log best-effort
357.         callback(finalContent, true);
358.         try { logMessage("out", sourceLabel, finalContent); } catch { /* best-effort */ }
359.         // Log both sides of the conversation after delivery
360.         try { logConversation(logRole, prompt, sourceLabel); } catch { /* best-effort */ }
361.         try { logConversation("assistant", finalContent, sourceLabel); } catch { /* best-effort */ }
362.         return;
363.       } catch (err) {
364.         const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
365. 
366.         // Don't retry cancelled messages
367.         if (/cancelled|abort/i.test(msg)) {
368.           return;
369.         }
370. 
371.         if (isRecoverableError(err) && attempt < MAX_RETRIES) {
372.           const delay = RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS[Math.min(attempt, RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS.length - 1)];
373.           console.error(`[max] Recoverable error: ${msg}. Retry ${attempt + 1}/${MAX_RETRIES} after ${delay}ms…`);
374.           await sleep(delay);
375.           // Reset client before retry in case the connection is stale
376.           try { await ensureClient(); } catch { /* will fail again on next attempt */ }
377.           continue;
378.         }
379. 
380.         console.error(`[max] Error processing message: ${msg}`);
381.         callback(`Error: ${msg}`, true);
382.         return;
383.       }
384.     }
385.   })();
386. }
387. 
388. /** Cancel the in-flight message and drain the queue. */
389. export async function cancelCurrentMessage(): Promise<boolean> {
390.   // Drain any queued messages
391.   const drained = messageQueue.length;
392.   while (messageQueue.length > 0) {
393.     const item = messageQueue.shift()!;
394.     item.reject(new Error("Cancelled"));
395.   }
396. 
397.   // Abort the active session request
398.   if (orchestratorSession && currentCallback) {
399.     try {
400.       await orchestratorSession.abort();
401.       console.log(`[max] Aborted in-flight request`);
402.       return true;
403.     } catch (err) {
404.       console.error(`[max] Abort failed:`, err instanceof Error ? err.message : err);
405.     }
406.   }
407. 
408.   return drained > 0;
409. }
410. 
411. export function getWorkers(): Map<string, WorkerInfo> {
412.   return workers;
413. }
414.

const C = {

  dim: (s: string) => `\x1b[2m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  cyan: (s: string) => `\x1b[36m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  green: (s: string) => `\x1b[32m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  yellow: (s: string) => `\x1b[33m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  red: (s: string) => `\x1b[31m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  magenta: (s: string) => `\x1b[35m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  boldCyan: (s: string) => `\x1b[1;36m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  bgDim: (s: string) => `\x1b[48;5;236m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  coral: (s: string) => `\x1b[38;2;255;127;80m${s}\x1b[0m`,
  boldWhite: (s: string) => `\x1b[1;97m${s}\x1b[0m`,

// ── Layout constants ─────────────────────────────────────

const TUI_DEBUG_ENABLED = /^(1|true|yes|on)$/i.test((process.env.MAX_TUI_DEBUG || "").trim());
let debugWriteFailureReported = false;

function previewForDebug(text: string, max = 120): string {
  return text
    .slice(0, max)
    .replace(/\r/g, "\\r")
    .replace(/\n/g, "\\n")
    .replace(/\t/g, "\\t");
}

function debugLog(event: string, data: Record<string, unknown> = {}): void {
  if (!TUI_DEBUG_ENABLED) return;
  const entry = {
    ts: new Date().toISOString(),
    event,
    ...data,
  };
  try {
    appendFileSync(TUI_DEBUG_LOG_PATH, JSON.stringify(entry) + "\n");
  } catch (err) {
    if (debugWriteFailureReported) return;
    debugWriteFailureReported = true;
    const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
    process.stderr.write(`\n[max] failed to write TUI debug log: ${msg}\n`);
  }
}

// ── Markdown → ANSI rendering ────────────────────────────

/** Render a single line of markdown to ANSI (used by both streaming and batch). */
function renderLine(line: string, inCodeBlock: boolean): string {
  if (inCodeBlock) {
    return `  ${C.dim("│")} ${line}`;
  }
  if (/^[-*_]{3,}\s*$/.test(line)) return C.dim("──────────────────────────────────");
  if (line.startsWith("### ")) return C.coral(line.slice(4));
  if (line.startsWith("## ")) return C.boldWhite(line.slice(3));
  if (line.startsWith("# ")) return C.boldWhite(line.slice(2));
  if (line.startsWith("> ")) return `${C.dim("│")} ${C.dim(line.slice(2))}`;
  if (/^ {2,}[-*] /.test(line)) return `    ◦ ${line.replace(/^ +[-*] /, "")}`;
  if (/^[-*] /.test(line)) return `  • ${line.slice(2)}`;
  if (/^\d+\. /.test(line)) return `  ${line}`;
  return line;
}

/** Apply inline formatting (bold, code, links, etc.) to already-rendered text. */
function applyInlineFormatting(text: string): string {
  return text
    .replace(/\*\*\*(.+?)\*\*\*/g, `\x1b[1;3m$1\x1b[0m`)
    .replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, `\x1b[1m$1\x1b[0m`)
    .replace(/~~(.+?)~~/g, `\x1b[9m$1\x1b[0m`)
    .replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, C.yellow("$1"))
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g, (_m, t, u) => `${t} ${C.dim(`(${u})`)}`);
}

/**
 * Copilot Session - represents a single conversation session with the Copilot CLI.
 * @module session
 */
import type { MessageConnection } from "vscode-jsonrpc/node";
import { createSessionRpc } from "./generated/rpc.js";
import type { MessageOptions, PermissionHandler, PermissionRequestResult, SessionEvent, SessionEventHandler, SessionEventType, SessionHooks, Tool, ToolHandler, TypedSessionEventHandler, UserInputHandler, UserInputResponse } from "./types.js";
/** Assistant message event - the final response from the assistant. */
export type AssistantMessageEvent = Extract<SessionEvent, {
    type: "assistant.message";
}>;
/**
 * Represents a single conversation session with the Copilot CLI.
 *
 * A session maintains conversation state, handles events, and manages tool execution.
 * Sessions are created via {@link CopilotClient.createSession} or resumed via
 * {@link CopilotClient.resumeSession}.
 *
 * @example
 * ```typescript
 * const session = await client.createSession({ model: "gpt-4" });
 *
 * // Subscribe to events
 * session.on((event) => {
 *   if (event.type === "assistant.message") {
 *     console.log(event.data.content);
 *   }
 * });
 *
 * // Send a message and wait for completion
 * await session.sendAndWait({ prompt: "Hello, world!" });
 *
 * // Clean up
 * await session.destroy();
 * ```
 */
export declare class CopilotSession {
    readonly sessionId: string;
    private connection;
    private readonly _workspacePath?;
    private eventHandlers;
    private typedEventHandlers;
    private toolHandlers;
    private permissionHandler?;
    private userInputHandler?;
    private hooks?;
    private _rpc;
    /**
     * Creates a new CopilotSession instance.
     *
     * @param sessionId - The unique identifier for this session
     * @param connection - The JSON-RPC message connection to the Copilot CLI
     * @param workspacePath - Path to the session workspace directory (when infinite sessions enabled)
     * @internal This constructor is internal. Use {@link CopilotClient.createSession} to create sessions.
     */
    constructor(sessionId: string, connection: MessageConnection, _workspacePath?: string | undefined);
    /**
     * Typed session-scoped RPC methods.
     */
    get rpc(): ReturnType<typeof createSessionRpc>;
    /**
     * Path to the session workspace directory when infinite sessions are enabled.
     * Contains checkpoints/, plan.md, and files/ subdirectories.
     * Undefined if infinite sessions are disabled.
     */
    get workspacePath(): string | undefined;
    /**
     * Sends a message to this session and waits for the response.
     *
     * The message is processed asynchronously. Subscribe to events via {@link on}
     * to receive streaming responses and other session events.
     *
     * @param options - The message options including the prompt and optional attachments
     * @returns A promise that resolves with the message ID of the response
     * @throws Error if the session has been destroyed or the connection fails
     *
     * @example
     * ```typescript
     * const messageId = await session.send({
     *   prompt: "Explain this code",
     *   attachments: [{ type: "file", path: "./src/index.ts" }]
     * });
     * ```
     */
    send(options: MessageOptions): Promise<string>;
    /**
     * Sends a message to this session and waits until the session becomes idle.
     *
     * This is a convenience method that combines {@link send} with waiting for
     * the `session.idle` event. Use this when you want to block until the
     * assistant has finished processing the message.
     *
     * Events are still delivered to handlers registered via {@link on} while waiting.
     *
     * @param options - The message options including the prompt and optional attachments
     * @param timeout - Timeout in milliseconds (default: 60000). Controls how long to wait; does not abort in-flight agent work.
     * @returns A promise that resolves with the final assistant message when the session becomes idle,
     *          or undefined if no assistant message was received
     * @throws Error if the timeout is reached before the session becomes idle
     * @throws Error if the session has been destroyed or the connection fails
     *
     * @example
     * ```typescript
     * // Send and wait for completion with default 60s timeout
     * const response = await session.sendAndWait({ prompt: "What is 2+2?" });
     * console.log(response?.data.content); // "4"
     * ```
     */
    sendAndWait(options: MessageOptions, timeout?: number): Promise<AssistantMessageEvent | undefined>;
    /**
     * Subscribes to events from this session.
     *
     * Events include assistant messages, tool executions, errors, and session state changes.
     * Multiple handlers can be registered and will all receive events.
     *
     * @param eventType - The specific event type to listen for (e.g., "assistant.message", "session.idle")
     * @param handler - A callback function that receives events of the specified type
     * @returns A function that, when called, unsubscribes the handler
     *
     * @example
     * ```typescript
     * // Listen for a specific event type
     * const unsubscribe = session.on("assistant.message", (event) => {
     *   console.log("Assistant:", event.data.content);
     * });
     *
     * // Later, to stop receiving events:
     * unsubscribe();
     * ```
     */
    on<K extends SessionEventType>(eventType: K, handler: TypedSessionEventHandler<K>): () => void;
    /**
     * Subscribes to all events from this session.
     *
     * @param handler - A callback function that receives all session events
     * @returns A function that, when called, unsubscribes the handler
     *
     * @example
     * ```typescript
     * const unsubscribe = session.on((event) => {
     *   switch (event.type) {
     *     case "assistant.message":
     *       console.log("Assistant:", event.data.content);
     *       break;
     *     case "session.error":
     *       console.error("Error:", event.data.message);
     *       break;
     *   }
     * });
     *
<exited with exit code 0>
````

export interface MessageOptions {
    /**
     * The prompt/message to send
     */
    prompt: string;
    /**
     * File, directory, or selection attachments
     */
    attachments?: Array<{
        type: "file";
        path: string;
        displayName?: string;
    } | {
        type: "directory";
        path: string;
        displayName?: string;
    } | {
        type: "selection";
        filePath: string;
        displayName: string;
        selection?: {
            start: {
                line: number;
                character: number;
            };
            end: {
                line: number;
                character: number;
            };
        };
        text?: string;
    }>;
    /**
     * Message delivery mode
     * - "enqueue": Add to queue (default)
     * - "immediate": Send immediately
     */
    mode?: "enqueue" | "immediate";
}

export type SessionEventHandler = (event: SessionEvent) => void;

  http.get(url, { headers: authHeaders() }, (res) =\> {

    if (event.type === "connected") {
      connectionId = event.connectionId;  // Line 395: CRITICAL — stores connection ID
      debugLog("sse-connected", { connectionId });
    }
  });

#### Message Sending (Lines 498-546):
```typescript
// Line 498-546: sendMessage() function
function sendMessage(prompt: string, requestId: number): void {
  const body = JSON.stringify({ prompt, connectionId });  // Line 499: REQUEST BODY
  const url = new URL("/message", API_BASE);
  
  const req = http.request(
    url,
    {
      method: "POST",  // Line 510
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "Content-Length": Buffer.byteLength(body),
        ...authHeaders(),
      },
    },
    (res) =\> {
      let data = "";
      res.on("data", (chunk) =\> (data += chunk));
      res.on("end", () =\> {
        if (res.statusCode !== 200) {
          stopThinking("message-post-error");
          console.error(C.red(`  Error: ${data}`));
          rl.prompt();
        }
      });
    }
  );
  
  req.on("error", (err) =\> {
    stopThinking("message-request-error");
    console.error(C.red(`  Failed to send: ${err.message}`));
  });
  
  req.write(body);  // Line 543
  req.end();
}
```

### 2. **API Endpoint** (`src/api/server.ts`)

#### POST /message Handler (Lines 94-121):
```typescript
// Line 94-121: POST /message endpoint
app.post("/message", (req: Request, res: Response) =\> {
  const { prompt, connectionId } = req.body as { 
    prompt?: string; 
    connectionId?: string 
  };

  // Line 97-100: Validate prompt
  if (!prompt || typeof prompt !== "string") {
    res.status(400).json({ error: "Missing 'prompt' in request body" });
    return;
  }

  // Line 102-105: Validate connectionId
  if (!connectionId || !sseClients.has(connectionId)) {
    res.status(400).json({ 
      error: "Missing or invalid 'connectionId'. Connect to /stream first." 
    });
    return;
  }

  // Line 107-118: Call sendToOrchestrator
  sendToOrchestrator(
    prompt,
    { type: "tui", connectionId },  // MessageSource with channel type
    (text: string, done: boolean) =\> {
      const sseRes = sseClients.get(connectionId);
      if (sseRes) {
        sseRes.write(
          `data: ${JSON.stringify({ 
            type: done ? "message" : "delta", 
            content: text 
          })}\n\n`
        );
      }
    }
  );

  res.json({ status: "queued" });  // Line 120
});
```

#### SSE Stream Endpoint (Lines 70-91):
```typescript
// Line 70-91: GET /stream — SSE connection handler
app.get("/stream", (req: Request, res: Response) =\> {
  const connectionId = `tui-${++connectionCounter}`;  // Line 71

  res.writeHead(200, {
    "Content-Type": "text/event-stream",
    "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
    Connection: "keep-alive",
  });
  res.write(
    `data: ${JSON.stringify({ type: "connected", connectionId })}\n\n`  // Line 78
  );

  sseClients.set(connectionId, res);  // Line 80: Store SSE response

  // Heartbeat to keep connection alive
  const heartbeat = setInterval(() =\> {
    res.write(`:ping\n\n`);
  }, 20_000);

  req.on("close", () =\> {
    clearInterval(heartbeat);
    sseClients.delete(connectionId);
  });
});
```

### 3. **Orchestrator** (`src/copilot/orchestrator.ts`)

#### sendToOrchestrator Function (Lines 325-386):
```typescript
// Line 325-386: sendToOrchestrator() — main entry point
export async function sendToOrchestrator(
  prompt: string,
  source: MessageSource,  // { type: "tui", connectionId }
  callback: MessageCallback  // (text: string, done: boolean) =\> void
): Promise\<void\> {
  const sourceLabel =
    source.type === "telegram" ? "telegram" :
    source.type === "tui" ? "tui" : "background";
  logMessage("in", sourceLabel, prompt);

  // Line 336-338: Tag the prompt with its source channel
  const taggedPrompt = source.type === "background"
    ? prompt
    : `[via ${sourceLabel}] ${prompt}`;

  // Line 344-346: Determine source channel for worker tracking
  const sourceChannel: "telegram" | "tui" | undefined =
    source.type === "telegram" ? "telegram" :
    source.type === "tui" ? "tui" : undefined;

  // Line 349-386: Async queue and retry logic
  void (async () =\> {
    for (let attempt = 0; attempt \<= MAX_RETRIES; attempt++) {
      try {
        const finalContent = await new Promise\<string\>((resolve, reject) =\> {
          messageQueue.push({ 
            prompt: taggedPrompt, 
            callback, 
            sourceChannel, 
            resolve, 
            reject 
          });
          processQueue();  // Process next in queue
        });
        
        callback(finalContent, true);  // Deliver final response
        logMessage("out", sourceLabel, finalContent);
        logConversation(logRole, prompt, sourceLabel);
        logConversation("assistant", finalContent, sourceLabel);
        return;
      } catch (err) {
        // Retry logic with exponential backoff
        if (isRecoverableError(err) && attempt \< MAX_RETRIES) {
          const delay = RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS[Math.min(attempt, RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS.length - 1)];
          console.error(`[max] Recoverable error: ${msg}. Retry ${attempt + 1}/${MAX_RETRIES} after ${delay}ms…`);
          await sleep(delay);
          await ensureClient();
          continue;
        }
        callback(`Error: ${msg}`, true);
        return;
      }
    }
  })();
}
```

#### executeOnSession Function (Lines 255-293):
```typescript
// Line 255-293: executeOnSession() — calls sendAndWait
async function executeOnSession(prompt: string, callback: MessageCallback): Promise\<string\> {
  const session = await ensureOrchestratorSession();
  currentCallback = callback;

  let accumulated = "";
  let toolCallExecuted = false;
  
  const unsubToolDone = session.on("tool.execution_complete", () =\> {
    toolCallExecuted = true;
  });
  
  const unsubDelta = session.on("assistant.message_delta", (event) =\> {
    if (toolCallExecuted && accumulated.length \> 0 && !accumulated.endsWith("\n")) {
      accumulated += "\n";
    }
    toolCallExecuted = false;
    accumulated += event.data.deltaContent;
    callback(accumulated, false);  // Stream deltas to TUI
  });

  try {
    // LINE 276: CRITICAL — sendAndWait call
    const result = await session.sendAndWait({ prompt }, 300_000);
    const finalContent = result?.data?.content || accumulated || "(No response)";
    return finalContent;
  } catch (err) {
    if (/closed|destroy|disposed|invalid|expired|not found/i.test(msg)) {
      orchestratorSession = undefined;
      deleteState(ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY);
    }
    throw err;
  } finally {
    unsubDelta();
    unsubToolDone();
    currentCallback = undefined;
  }
}
```

}, 60_000);

### 4. **SDK Types** (`@github/copilot-sdk/dist/types.d.ts`)

#### sendAndWait Method Signature:
```typescript
/**
 * Sends a message to this session and waits until the session becomes idle.
 * 
 * This is a convenience method that combines send() with waiting for
 * the `session.idle` event. Use this when you want to block until the
 * assistant has finished processing the message.
 * 
 * @param options - The message options including the prompt and optional attachments
 * @param timeout - Timeout in milliseconds (default: 60000)
 * @returns A promise that resolves with the final assistant message when the 
 *          session becomes idle, or undefined if no assistant message was received
 * @throws Error if the timeout is reached before the session becomes idle
 * @throws Error if the session has been destroyed or the connection fails
 * 
 * @example
 * const response = await session.sendAndWait({ prompt: "What is 2+2?" });
 * console.log(response?.data.content); // "4"
 */
sendAndWait(options: MessageOptions, timeout?: number): Promise\<AssistantMessageEvent | undefined\>;
```

#### MessageOptions Interface:
```typescript
export interface MessageOptions {
  /**
   * The prompt/message to send
   */
  prompt: string;

  /**
   * File, directory, or selection attachments
   */
  attachments?: Array\<
    | {
        type: "file";
        path: string;
        displayName?: string;
      }
    | {
        type: "directory";
        path: string;
        displayName?: string;
      }
    | {
        type: "selection";
        filePath: string;
        displayName: string;
        selection?: {
          start: {
            line: number;
            character: number;
          };
          end: {
            line: number;
            character: number;
          };
        };
        text?: string;
      }
  \>;

  /**
   * Message delivery mode
   * - "enqueue": Add to queue (default)
   * - "immediate": Send immediately
   */
  mode?: "enqueue" | "immediate";
}
```

#### AssistantMessageEvent Return Type:
```typescript
// Inferred from SessionEvent discriminated union:
type AssistantMessageEvent = Extract\<SessionEvent, {
  type: "assistant.message";
}\>;

// Contains: 
// - event.type = "assistant.message"
// - event.data.content = string (the final response)
// - event.data.messageId = string
```

## Summary: Complete Message Flow

```
TUI Input (stdin)
    ↓
rl.on("line", handler)
    ↓
sendMessage(prompt, requestId)
    │   Uses stored connectionId from SSE /stream
    ↓
HTTP POST /message
    Body: { prompt, connectionId }
    ↓
API Handler: sendToOrchestrator(prompt, source, callback)
    source = { type: "tui", connectionId }
    ↓
Message Queue → executeOnSession(prompt, callback)
    ↓
session.sendAndWait({ prompt }, 300_000)
    │   Waits for session.idle event (max 5 minutes)
    │   Streams deltas via assistant.message_delta events
    ↓
Result received → callback(finalContent, true)
    ↓
Sent via SSE to TUI: { type: "message", content: text }
    ↓
TUI renders response
```

247.   try {
248.     await ensureOrchestratorSession();
249.   } catch (err) {
250.     console.error(`[max] Failed to create initial session (will retry on first message):`, err instanceof Error ? err.message : err);
251.   }
252. }
253. 
254. /** Send a prompt on the persistent session, return the response. */
255. async function executeOnSession(prompt: string, callback: MessageCallback): Promise<string> {
256.   const session = await ensureOrchestratorSession();
257.   currentCallback = callback;
258. 
259.   let accumulated = "";
260.   let toolCallExecuted = false;
261.   const unsubToolDone = session.on("tool.execution_complete", () => {
262.     toolCallExecuted = true;
263.   });
264.   const unsubDelta = session.on("assistant.message_delta", (event) => {
265.     // After a tool call completes, ensure a line break separates the text blocks
266.     // so they don't visually run together in the TUI.
267.     if (toolCallExecuted && accumulated.length > 0 && !accumulated.endsWith("\n")) {
268.       accumulated += "\n";
269.     }
270.     toolCallExecuted = false;
271.     accumulated += event.data.deltaContent;
272.     callback(accumulated, false);
273.   });
274. 
275.   try {
276.     const result = await session.sendAndWait({ prompt }, 300_000);
277.     const finalContent = result?.data?.content || accumulated || "(No response)";
278.     return finalContent;
279.   } catch (err) {
280.     // If the session is broken, invalidate it so it's recreated on next attempt
281.     const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
282.     if (/closed|destroy|disposed|invalid|expired|not found/i.test(msg)) {
283.       console.log(`[max] Session appears dead, will recreate: ${msg}`);
284.       orchestratorSession = undefined;
285.       deleteState(ORCHESTRATOR_SESSION_KEY);
286.     }
287.     throw err;
288.   } finally {
289.     unsubDelta();
290.     unsubToolDone();
291.     currentCallback = undefined;
292.   }
293. }
294. 
295. /** Process the message queue one at a time. */
296. async function processQueue(): Promise<void> {
297.   if (processing) {
298.     if (messageQueue.length > 0) {
299.       console.log(`[max] Message queued (${messageQueue.length} waiting — orchestrator is busy)`);
300.     }
301.     return;
302.   }
303.   processing = true;
304. 
305.   while (messageQueue.length > 0) {
306.     const item = messageQueue.shift()!;
307.     currentSourceChannel = item.sourceChannel;
308.     try {
309.       const result = await executeOnSession(item.prompt, item.callback);
310.       item.resolve(result);
311.     } catch (err) {
312.       item.reject(err);
313.     }
314.     currentSourceChannel = undefined;
315.   }
316. 
317.   processing = false;
318. }
319. 
320. function isRecoverableError(err: unknown): boolean {
321.   const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
322.   return /timeout|disconnect|connection|EPIPE|ECONNRESET|ECONNREFUSED|socket|closed|ENOENT|spawn|not found|expired|stale/i.test(msg);
323. }
324. 
325. export async function sendToOrchestrator(
326.   prompt: string,
327.   source: MessageSource,
328.   callback: MessageCallback
329. ): Promise<void> {
330.   const sourceLabel =
331.     source.type === "telegram" ? "telegram" :
332.     source.type === "tui" ? "tui" : "background";
333.   logMessage("in", sourceLabel, prompt);
334. 
335.   // Tag the prompt with its source channel
336.   const taggedPrompt = source.type === "background"
337.     ? prompt
338.     : `[via ${sourceLabel}] ${prompt}`;
339. 
340.   // Log role: background events are "system", user messages are "user"
341.   const logRole = source.type === "background" ? "system" : "user";
342. 
343.   // Determine the source channel for worker origin tracking
344.   const sourceChannel: "telegram" | "tui" | undefined =
345.     source.type === "telegram" ? "telegram" :
346.     source.type === "tui" ? "tui" : undefined;
347. 
348.   // Enqueue and process
349.   void (async () => {
350.     for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= MAX_RETRIES; attempt++) {
351.       try {
352.         const finalContent = await new Promise<string>((resolve, reject) => {
353.           messageQueue.push({ prompt: taggedPrompt, callback, sourceChannel, resolve, reject });
354.           processQueue();
355.         });
356.         // Deliver response to user FIRST, then log best-effort
357.         callback(finalContent, true);
358.         try { logMessage("out", sourceLabel, finalContent); } catch { /* best-effort */ }
359.         // Log both sides of the conversation after delivery
360.         try { logConversation(logRole, prompt, sourceLabel); } catch { /* best-effort */ }
361.         try { logConversation("assistant", finalContent, sourceLabel); } catch { /* best-effort */ }
362.         return;
363.       } catch (err) {
364.         const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
365. 
366.         // Don't retry cancelled messages
367.         if (/cancelled|abort/i.test(msg)) {
368.           return;
369.         }
370. 
371.         if (isRecoverableError(err) && attempt < MAX_RETRIES) {
372.           const delay = RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS[Math.min(attempt, RECONNECT_DELAYS_MS.length - 1)];
373.           console.error(`[max] Recoverable error: ${msg}. Retry ${attempt + 1}/${MAX_RETRIES} after ${delay}ms…`);
374.           await sleep(delay);
375.           // Reset client before retry in case the connection is stale
376.           try { await ensureClient(); } catch { /* will fail again on next attempt */ }
377.           continue;
378.         }
379. 
380.         console.error(`[max] Error processing message: ${msg}`);
381.         callback(`Error: ${msg}`, true);
382.         return;
383.       }
384.     }
385.   })();
386. }
387. 
388. /** Cancel the in-flight message and drain the queue. */
389. export async function cancelCurrentMessage(): Promise<boolean> {
390.   // Drain any queued messages
391.   const drained = messageQueue.length;
392.   while (messageQueue.length > 0) {
393.     const item = messageQueue.shift()!;
394.     item.reject(new Error("Cancelled"));
395.   }
396. 
397.   // Abort the active session request
398.   if (orchestratorSession && currentCallback) {
399.     try {
400.       await orchestratorSession.abort();
401.       console.log(`[max] Aborted in-flight request`);
402.       return true;
403.     } catch (err) {
404.       console.error(`[max] Abort failed:`, err instanceof Error ? err.message : err);
405.     }
406.   }
407. 
408.   return drained > 0;
409. }
410. 
411. export function getWorkers(): Map<string, WorkerInfo> {
412.   return workers;
413. }
414.
```

### 💬 Copilot

Build passes. Here's a summary of all changes across 3 files:

**`src/copilot/orchestrator.ts`** — Added `FileAttachment` type and threaded `attachments?` through `sendToOrchestrator()` → message queue → `executeOnSession()` → `session.sendAndWait()`

**`src/api/server.ts`** — POST `/message` now accepts an `attachments` array in the body. Validates each attachment has a valid image extension and exists on disk before forwarding.

**`src/tui/index.ts`** — Two ways to attach images:
1. **`/image \<path\> [prompt]`** — explicit command
2. **Auto-detection** — image file paths (`.png`, `.jpg`, etc.) in regular messages are automatically detected as attachments (supports quoted, escaped-space, and plain paths)

Both show a `📎 filename` indicator when images are attached. Help text updated accordingly.

+// ── Image attachment parsing ─────────────────────────────
+const IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = new Set([".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".gif", ".webp", ".bmp"]);
+
+type ImageAttachment = { type: "file"; path: string; displayName: string };
+
+/**
+ * Parse image file paths from user input. Handles:
+ * - Quoted paths: "/path/to/my image.png" or '/path/to/my image.png'
+ * - Escaped spaces: /path/to/my\ image.png
+m * - Plain paths: /path/to/image.png or ./relative/image.png
+ * Returns the remaining prompt text and any detected image attachments.
+ */
+function parseImageAttachments(input: string): { prompt: string; attachments: ImageAttachment[] } {
+  const attachments: ImageAttachment[] = [];
+  let remaining = input;
+
+  // Match double-quoted paths: "..."
+  const dblQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)"([^"]*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))"/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(dblQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
+    const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  // Match single-quoted paths: '...'
+  const sglQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)'([^']*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))'/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(sglQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
+    const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  // Match escaped-space paths: tokens with backslash-escaped spaces
+  const escapedPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:[^\s"'\\]|\\.)*\\[ ](?:[^\s"'\\]|\\.)*\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(escapedPattern, (_match, rawPath) => {
+    const unescaped = rawPath.replace(/\\ /g, " ");
+    const resolved = path.resolve(unescaped);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  // Match plain paths: no spaces, start with / or ./ or ~/ or alphanumeric
+  const plainPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:~\/|\.\/|\.\.\/|\/|[a-zA-Z]:[\\/])?[^\s"']+\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))(?=\s|$)/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(plainPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
+    const expanded = filePath.startsWith("~/")
+      ? path.join(process.env.HOME || "", filePath.slice(2))
+      : filePath;
+    const resolved = path.resolve(expanded);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  return { prompt: remaining.replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim(), attachments };
+}

$ cd /Users/burkeholland/dev/max && node -e "
// Create test file to verify actual behavior
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

// Create the parseImageAttachments function exactly as in the code
const IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = new Set(['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.webp', '.bmp']);

function parseImageAttachments(input) {
  const attachments = [];
  let remaining = input;

  // Match double-quoted paths
  const dblQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)\"([^\"]*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))\"/gi;
  remaining = remaining.replace(dblQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
    const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
    if (fs.existsSync(resolved)) {
      attachments.push({ type: 'file', path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
      return '';
    }
    return _match;
  });

  // Match single-quoted paths
  const sglQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)'([^']*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))'/gi;
  remaining = remaining.replace(sglQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
    const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
    if (fs.existsSync(resolved)) {
      attachments.push({ type: 'file', path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
      return '';
    }
    return _match;
  });

  // Match escaped-space paths
  const escapedPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:[^\s\"'\\\\]|\\\\.)*\\\\[ ](?:[^\s\"'\\\\]|\\\\.)*\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))/gi;
  remaining = remaining.replace(escapedPattern, (_match, rawPath) => {
    const unescaped = rawPath.replace(/\\\\ /g, ' ');
    const resolved = path.resolve(unescaped);
    if (fs.existsSync(resolved)) {
      attachments.push({ type: 'file', path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
      return '';
    }
    return _match;
  });

  // Match plain paths
  const plainPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:~\/|\.\/|\.\.\/|\/|[a-zA-Z]:[\\\\/])?[^\s\"']+\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))(?=\s|\$)/gi;
  remaining = remaining.replace(plainPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
    const expanded = filePath.startsWith('~/')
      ? path.join(process.env.HOME || '', filePath.slice(2))
      : filePath;
    const resolved = path.resolve(expanded);
    if (fs.existsSync(resolved)) {
      attachments.push({ type: 'file', path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
      return '';
    }
    return _match;
  });

  return { prompt: remaining.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(), attachments };
}

  });

+// ── Image attachment parsing ─────────────────────────────
+const IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = new Set([".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".gif", ".webp", ".bmp"]);
+
+type ImageAttachment = { type: "file"; path: string; displayName: string };
+
+/**
+ * Parse image file paths from user input. Handles:
+ * - Quoted paths: "/path/to/my image.png" or '/path/to/my image.png'
+ * - Escaped spaces: /path/to/my\ image.png
+ * - Plain paths: /path/to/image.png or ./relative/image.png
+ * Returns the remaining prompt text and any detected image attachments.
+ */
+function parseImageAttachments(input: string): { prompt: string; attachments: ImageAttachment[] } {
+  const attachments: ImageAttachment[] = [];
+  let remaining = input;
+
+  // Match double-quoted paths: "..."
+  const dblQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)"([^"]*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))"/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(dblQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
+    const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  // Match single-quoted paths: '...'
+  const sglQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)'([^']*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))'/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(sglQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
+    const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  // Match escaped-space paths: tokens with backslash-escaped spaces
+  const escapedPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:[^\s"'\\]|\\.)*\\[ ](?:[^\s"'\\]|\\.)*\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))/gi;
+  remaining = remaining.replace(escapedPattern, (_match, rawPath) => {
+    const unescaped = rawPath.replace(/\\ /g, " ");
+    const resolved = path.resolve(unescaped);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+
+  // Match plain paths: no spaces, start with / or ./ or ~/ or alphanumeric
+  const plainPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:~\/|\.\/|\.\.\/|\/|[a-zA-Z]:[\\/])?[^\s"']+\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))(?=\s|$)/gi;

+      ? path.join(process.env.HOME || "", filePath.slice(2))

+    const resolved = path.resolve(expanded);
+    if (existsSync(resolved)) {
+      attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
+      return "";
+    }
+    return _match;
+  });
+

Let me write my findings:

## Issue: Path Traversal Vulnerability in Image Attachment Feature
**File:** src/tui/index.ts:92-96 and src/tui/index.ts:935-945
**Severity:** Critical
**Problem:** The code accepts user-provided file paths without validating that they stay within safe boundaries. Users can supply paths like `../../../etc/passwd.png` or `~/../../../etc/passwd.png` which resolve to arbitrary filesystem locations. While the API server checks if files exist (line 128 of server.ts), there's no validation preventing access to sensitive files outside the intended working directory.

**Evidence:** Tested path resolution behavior:
- Input: `../../../etc/passwd.png` → Resolves to `/Users/etc/passwd.png` (escapes project directory)
- Input: `~/../../etc/passwd.png` → Resolves to `/etc/passwd.png` after tilde expansion
- Input: `~/../../../etc/passwd.png` → Resolves to `/etc/passwd.png`

The tilde expansion at lines 93-95 of tui/index.ts is particularly dangerous:
```typescript
const expanded = filePath.startsWith("~/")
  ? path.join(process.env.HOME || "", filePath.slice(2))
  : filePath;
```
This allows `~/../../etc/passwd.png` to traverse outside HOME after the join.

**Suggested fix:** Add path validation after resolution to ensure the resolved path is within allowed directories (e.g., user's HOME, current working directory, or specific allowed upload directories). Use something like:
```typescript
const resolved = path.resolve(expanded);
const allowedDirs = [process.cwd(), process.env.HOME];
if (!allowedDirs.some(dir =\> resolved.startsWith(path.resolve(dir)))) {
  throw new Error('Path outside allowed directories');
}
```

---

## Issue: Multiple Duplicate Attachment Risk
**File:** src/tui/index.ts:1015-1022
**Severity:** Medium
**Problem:** When a user sends a normal prompt (not using `/image` command), the code runs `parseImageAttachments()` to auto-detect image paths. However, if the same input is processed by both the regex patterns and later sent through the API, there's potential for duplicate processing or unexpected behavior. More critically, the auto-detection at line 1015 applies the same path traversal vulnerability to ALL user messages without any command prefix needed.

**Evidence:** At line 1015, every user input goes through `parseImageAttachments()`:
```typescript
const parsed = parseImageAttachments(trimmed);
```
This means typing `../../../etc/passwd.png what is this` would auto-attach that file without explicit `/image` command.

**Suggested fix:** Either remove auto-detection from normal messages and require explicit `/image` command, OR clearly document this behavior and ensure path validation is in place before any auto-detection runs.

---

## Issue: Missing Error Handling for File Read Operations
**File:** src/api/server.ts:128 and src/copilot/orchestrator.ts:285
**Severity:** High
**Problem:** The API server validates that files exist (line 128: `existsSync(att.path)`) but doesn't validate file permissions or handle the case where the file becomes unreadable between the existence check and when the Copilot SDK tries to read it (TOCTOU - Time-of-check-time-of-use race condition). Additionally, there's no error handling if `session.sendAndWait()` fails due to file read errors.

**Evidence:** The flow is:
1. Line 128 (server.ts): Check file exists
2. Line 132: Add to attachments array  
3. Line 285 (orchestrator.ts): Pass directly to `session.sendAndWait()`

No error handling exists for:
- Permission denied errors when SDK tries to read the file
- File deleted/moved between validation and reading
- File too large or corrupted
- File type mismatch (e.g., not actually an image despite extension)

**Suggested fix:** Add try-catch around the `sendAndWait` call with specific error handling for file-related errors. Consider validating file readability and size limits in the API server before accepting the attachment.

---

## Issue: Type Safety Gap in Attachment Flow
**File:** src/copilot/orchestrator.ts:283-285
**Severity:** Medium
**Problem:** The code conditionally adds `attachments` to the options object only if the array has length \> 0, but the TypeScript type for `sendOpts` doesn't match what the Copilot SDK actually expects. There's an implicit assumption that the SDK's `sendAndWait()` method accepts a `FileAttachment` type that matches the locally defined type, but there's no import or type checking to verify this.

**Evidence:** At line 285:
```typescript
const sendOpts: { prompt: string; attachments?: FileAttachment[] } = { prompt };
if (attachments && attachments.length \> 0) sendOpts.attachments = attachments;
const result = await session.sendAndWait(sendOpts, 300_000);
```

The `FileAttachment` type is defined locally (lines 23-27) but there's no verification that it matches what the Copilot SDK expects. If the SDK expects different properties (e.g., `filePath` instead of `path`, or requires additional metadata), this will fail at runtime.

**Suggested fix:** Import the attachment type from the Copilot SDK if available, or add runtime validation to ensure the attachment objects match the expected shape before passing to the SDK.


---

**`src/api/server.ts`** — POST `/message` now accepts an `attachments` array. Validates each attachment has a supported image extension (`.png`, `.jpg`, `.jpeg`, `.gif`, `.webp`, `.bmp`) and exists on disk.

**`src/tui/index.ts`** — Two complementary input methods:
1. **`/image <path> [prompt]`** — Explicit command for image attachment

Agent completed. agent_id: agent-3, agent_type: code-review, status: completed, description: GPT 5.4 code review, elapsed: 129s, model: gpt-5.4, duration: 121s

Result:
## Issue: Malformed `attachments` payloads can return 500s instead of a validation error
**File:** `src/api/server.ts:116`
**Severity:** Medium  
**Problem:** The new validation loop assumes every array element is a non-null object. A request like `{"attachments":[null]}` will throw on `att.type` before the route can reject it, so the API returns an internal error instead of a clean 400. Also, if `attachments` is present but not an array, it is silently ignored and the message is processed without the intended file.
**Evidence:** The route only enters validation for `Array.isArray(rawAttachments)`, then immediately dereferences `att.type` and `att.path`. Reproduced with a Node snippet: iterating `[null]` through this logic throws `Cannot read properties of null (reading 'type')`.
**Suggested fix:** Reject any non-array `attachments` value when the field is present, and validate each element is a non-null object before reading `type`/`path`.

## Issue: `~/...` image paths fail when quoted or escaped
**File:** `src/tui/index.ts:57`, `src/tui/index.ts:80`, `src/tui/index.ts:933`
**Severity:** Medium  
**Problem:** Home-relative paths are only expanded in the plain-path branch. Quoted paths (`"~/Pictures/my image.png"`) and escaped-space paths (`~/Pictures/my\ image.png`) are sent through `path.resolve()` without `~` expansion, so they resolve to `<cwd>/~/...` and are never attached. That breaks a common way users enter paths with spaces, especially via `/image`.
**Evidence:** In the parser, only the plain matcher does `filePath.startsWith("~/") ? path.join(process.env.HOME...) : filePath`. The quoted and escaped branches call `path.resolve(...)` directly. Reproduced with a temp file in `$HOME`: `~/max-test-image.png` is detected, but `"~/max test image.png"` and `~/max\ test\ image.png` both return zero attachments.
**Suggested fix:** Normalize `~` expansion in one shared helper and use it in every parser branch, including the `/image` fallback path parsing.
```

</details>

Agent completed. agent_id: agent-4, agent_type: code-review, status: completed, description: Sonnet 4.6 code review, elapsed: 293s, model: claude-sonnet-4.6, duration: 293s

Result:
---

## Issue: `/image` fallback produces wrong error for quoted and escaped-space paths

**File:** `src/tui/index.ts:936`
**Severity:** Medium

**Problem:** The fallback block (lines 934–953), which runs when `parseImageAttachments` finds no existing file, unconditionally splits `imageArg` on whitespace to get `rawPath`:

```ts
const rawPath = imageArg.split(/\s+/)[0];
```

This assumption breaks for every input syntax other than plain unquoted paths:

- **Quoted path, no spaces** — `/image "/nonexistent/image.png"`: `rawPath` becomes `"/nonexistent/image.png"` (with the literal `"` prefix). `path.extname` then returns `.png"` (the closing quote is included), which fails the `IMAGE_EXTENSIONS` check, so the user gets `Unsupported format: .png"` instead of `File not found`.

- **Quoted path, with spaces** — `/image "/nonexistent/my image.png"`: `rawPath` becomes `"/nonexistent/my` (stops at the space). `path.extname` returns `""`, so the user gets `Unsupported format: (none)`.

- **Escaped-space path** — `/image /nonexistent/my\ image.png`: `rawPath` becomes `/nonexistent/my\` (stops at the escaped-space). Again `ext` is `""` → `Unsupported format: (none)`.

**Evidence:** Verified with Node.js:
```
rawPath: "/path/to/nonexistent.png"   ext: .png"    ← includes closing quote
rawPath: "/path/to/my                 ext:           ← empty, splits at space
```

The fallback is only correct for plain unquoted paths. For the other three syntaxes the parser explicitly handles (double-quoted, single-quoted, escaped-space), a nonexistent file always produces a misleading "Unsupported format" error rather than "File not found".

**Suggested fix:** The fallback should check whether `imageArg` begins with a quote or contains an escaped space and extract the path accordingly — using the same logic already present in `parseImageAttachments` — before calling `path.extname`.
````

</details>

Agent completed. agent_id: agent-2, agent_type: code-review, status: completed, description: Opus code review, elapsed: 380s, model: claude-opus-4.6, duration: 380s

Result:
## Issue: Missing tilde (`~`) expansion in quoted and escaped path handlers
**File:** /Users/burkeholland/dev/max/src/tui/index.ts:59, 70, 82
**Severity:** Medium
**Problem:** The double-quoted, single-quoted, and escaped-space path handlers pass the captured path directly to `path.resolve()` without expanding a leading `~/`. Only the plain-path handler (line 93) performs tilde expansion. `path.resolve("~/Pictures/photo.jpg")` resolves to `$CWD/~/Pictures/photo.jpg` (a literal `~` directory), not the user's home directory.

This means any tilde path that *requires* quoting or escaping—i.e., paths with spaces—will always fail the `existsSync` check and silently not attach. Example: `"~/My Pictures/screenshot.png"` or `~/My\ Pictures/screenshot.png` will never work, even when the file exists.

**Evidence:** Verified in Node.js:
```
path.resolve("~/Pictures/photo.jpg")
→ "/Users/burkeholland/dev/max/~/Pictures/photo.jpg"  // wrong

path.resolve(path.join(process.env.HOME, "Pictures/photo.jpg"))
→ "/Users/burkeholland/Pictures/photo.jpg"             // correct
```

**Suggested fix:** Apply the same tilde expansion (`startsWith("~/") ? path.join(process.env.HOME, ...) : ...`) before `path.resolve()` in the double-quoted handler (line 59), single-quoted handler (line 70), and escaped-space handler (line 82), matching what the plain handler already does at line 93.
````

</details>

---

### 🔍 Review Summary (3 models)

| # | Issue | Found By | Severity |
|---|-------|----------|----------|
| 1 | **Missing `~` expansion in quoted/escaped path handlers** | Opus, GPT 5.4 | Medium |
| 2 | **`/image` fallback misparsing quoted/escaped paths** | Sonnet 4.6 | Medium |
| 3 | **Malformed `attachments` payload crashes with 500** | GPT 5.4 | Medium |

**Issue 1** (consensus: Opus + GPT 5.4): Tilde (`~/`) expansion only happens in the plain-path regex branch. Quoted paths like `"~/My Photos/img.png"` and escaped paths like `~/My\ Photos/img.png` resolve to `\<cwd\>/~/...` instead of the home directory.

**Issue 2** (Sonnet 4.6): The `/image` fallback does `imageArg.split(/\s+/)[0]` which breaks on quoted and escaped-space paths, producing misleading error messages like `Unsupported format: .png"`.

**Issue 3** (GPT 5.4): A request with `"attachments": [null]` throws an unhandled error. Non-array `attachments` values are silently ignored.

All three are real bugs. Let me fix them.

### ✅ `view`

/Users/burkeholland/dev/max/src/tui/index.ts (lines 39-105)

<details>
<summary>67 lines</summary>

```
39. 
40. // ── Image attachment parsing ─────────────────────────────
41. const IMAGE_EXTENSIONS = new Set([".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".gif", ".webp", ".bmp"]);
42. 
43. type ImageAttachment = { type: "file"; path: string; displayName: string };
44. 
45. /**
46.  * Parse image file paths from user input. Handles:
47.  * - Quoted paths: "/path/to/my image.png" or '/path/to/my image.png'
48.  * - Escaped spaces: /path/to/my\ image.png
49.  * - Plain paths: /path/to/image.png or ./relative/image.png
50.  * Returns the remaining prompt text and any detected image attachments.
51.  */
52. function parseImageAttachments(input: string): { prompt: string; attachments: ImageAttachment[] } {
53.   const attachments: ImageAttachment[] = [];
54.   let remaining = input;
55. 
56.   // Match double-quoted paths: "..."
57.   const dblQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)"([^"]*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))"/gi;
58.   remaining = remaining.replace(dblQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
59.     const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
60.     if (existsSync(resolved)) {
61.       attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
62.       return "";
63.     }
64.     return _match;
65.   });
66. 
67.   // Match single-quoted paths: '...'
68.   const sglQuotedPattern = /(?:^|\s)'([^']*?\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))'/gi;
69.   remaining = remaining.replace(sglQuotedPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
70.     const resolved = path.resolve(filePath);
71.     if (existsSync(resolved)) {
72.       attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
73.       return "";
74.     }
75.     return _match;
76.   });
77. 
78.   // Match escaped-space paths: tokens with backslash-escaped spaces
79.   const escapedPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:[^\s"'\\]|\\.)*\\[ ](?:[^\s"'\\]|\\.)*\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))/gi;
80.   remaining = remaining.replace(escapedPattern, (_match, rawPath) => {
81.     const unescaped = rawPath.replace(/\\ /g, " ");
82.     const resolved = path.resolve(unescaped);
83.     if (existsSync(resolved)) {
84.       attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
85.       return "";
86.     }
87.     return _match;
88.   });
89. 
90.   // Match plain paths: no spaces, start with / or ./ or ~/ or alphanumeric
91.   const plainPattern = /(?:^|\s)((?:~\/|\.\/|\.\.\/|\/|[a-zA-Z]:[\\/])?[^\s"']+\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|bmp))(?=\s|$)/gi;
92.   remaining = remaining.replace(plainPattern, (_match, filePath) => {
93.     const expanded = filePath.startsWith("~/")
94.       ? path.join(process.env.HOME || "", filePath.slice(2))
95.       : filePath;
96.     const resolved = path.resolve(expanded);
97.     if (existsSync(resolved)) {
98.       attachments.push({ type: "file", path: resolved, displayName: path.basename(resolved) });
99.       return "";
100.     }
101.     return _match;
102.   });
103. 
104.   return { prompt: remaining.replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim(), attachments };
105. }
```

144.         );
145.       }
```
